***sullen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sullen.html>sullen</a> (32261)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sulan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skulaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:sullen.html>sullen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> must, to have to</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> negated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> may, be allowed to</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> will, shall, be going to <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">future tense</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1249</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Schepenbrief_van_Bochoute" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Schepenbrief van Bochoute">Schepenbrief <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Bochoute</a></cite>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Velzeke" class="extiw" title="w:Velzeke">Velzeke</a>, eastern <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/County_of_Flanders" class="extiw" title="w:County of Flanders">Flanders</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="dum">Descepenen <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> bochouta quedden <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:degene.html>degene</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dese.html>dese</a> lettren sien <b><a href = vnd.unilang:selen.html>selen</a></b> i(n) onsen here.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The aldermen of Bochoute address all who <b>will</b> see this letter by our lord.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in the past tense</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be about to <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">inchoative</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">modal  auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">indicates a possible or hypothetical situation</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">modal  auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">indicates information garnered from a third party that may or may not be reliable</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a> (18156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/First_Rain_%28228226305%29.jpg/220px-First_Rain_%28228226305%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/First_Rain_%28228226305%29.jpg/330px-First_Rain_%28228226305%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/First_Rain_%28228226305%29.jpg/440px-First_Rain_%28228226305%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3456" data-file-height="2304" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A child whose face and hand have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> sullied after playing with mud</div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sulen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sulien</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to become dirty; to defile, pollute, taint</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sylian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to soil, pollute; to <a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*suliwōną</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sulwōną</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sulwijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make dirty; to <a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sūl-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thick liquid, muck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perhaps conflated partially with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">souillier</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to soil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">souiller</i>) from the same Germanic source. The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">søle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">zaluwen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">saluwen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">sühlen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">sulian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">söla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i>Also compare</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sulpen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to defile, pollute</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">solian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to soil, become defiled, make or become foul</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <i>see more</i> at <span class="Latn" lang="en">soil</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">sullies</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sullying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sullied</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To soil or stain; to dirty.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">sowl</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not wish to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></b> his hands with gardening.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1672</b>,  The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Earl_of_Roscommon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Earl of Roscommon"><a href = vnd.unilang:earl.html>Earl</a> of Roscommon</a>  | <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wentworth_Dillon,_4th_Earl_of_Roscommon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wentworth Dillon, 4th Earl of Roscommon">Wentworth Dillon, 4th <a href = vnd.unilang:earl.html>Earl</a> of Roscommon</a> | ,  “The Sixth <a href = vnd.unilang:ode.html>Ode</a>, of the Third Book of <i>Horace</i>”, in  <cite>Poems by the <a href = vnd.unilang:earl.html>Earl</a> of Roscomon</cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacob_Tonson" class="extiw" title="w:Jacob Tonson">J[acob] Tonson</a>, published 1717, lines 1–6, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/earlofros00roscpage/153">page 153</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">THoſe Ills your Anceſtors have done, / <i>Romans,</i> are now become your own ; / And they will coſt you dear, / Unleſs you ſoon repair / The falling Temples which the <a href = vnd.unilang:gods.html>Gods</a> provoke, / And Statues <b>ſully’d</b> yet with Sacrilegious Smoke.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1826</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Fenimore_Cooper" class="extiw" title="w:James Fenimore Cooper">[James Fenimore <a href = vnd.unilang:cooper.html>Cooper</a>]</a>,  chapter I, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Last_of_the_Mohicans" class="extiw" title="w:The Last of the Mohicans">The Last of the Mohicans; a Narrative of 1757. <span style="font-style: normal;">[...]</span> In Two <a href = vnd.unilang:volumes.html>Volumes</a></a></cite>, volume I, Philadelphia, <a href = vnd.unilang:pa.html>Pa</a>. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Charles_Carey" class="extiw" title="w:Henry Charles Carey">H[enry] C[harles] Carey</a> amp; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Lea" class="extiw" title="w:Isaac Lea">I[saac] Lea</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chestnut_Street_(Philadelphia)" class="extiw" title="w:Chestnut Street (Philadelphia)">Chestnut-Street</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/1538219">1538219</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=uthEAQAAMAAJamp;pg=PA10">page 10</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">His nether garment <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> of yellow nankeen, closely fitted to the shape, and tied at his bunches of knees by large <a href = vnd.unilang:knots.html>knots</a> of white ribbon, a good deal <b>sullied</b> by use.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To corrupt or damage.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">She tried to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></b> her rival’s reputation with a suggestive comment.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2010</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ken_Gormley_(academic)" class="extiw" title="w:Ken Gormley (academic)"><a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>Ken</a> Gormley</a>,  “One Nation Divided”, in  <cite>The Death of American Virtue: Clinton <a href = vnd.unilang:vs.html>vs</a>. Starr</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crown_Publishing_Group" class="extiw" title="w:Crown Publishing Group">Crown Publishers</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=MkwPI8pFmm0Camp;pg=PA431">page 431</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ken_Starr" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ken Starr"><a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>Ken</a> Starr</a> would <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> conclude that it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a mistake for him to expand into the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Monica_Lewinsky" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Monica Lewinsky"><a href = vnd.unilang:monica.html>Monica</a> Lewinsky</a> matter, largely because of the disastrous impact it would have on his <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Whitewater_controversy" class="extiw" title="w:Whitewater controversy">Whitewater/Madison</a> investigation and in <b>sullying</b> his otherwise sterling professional reputation.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  Dedra Mcdonald Birzer,  “To Delight in Sacrifice: True Love in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:jane.html>Jane</a> Eyre</i>”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charlotte_Bront%C3%AB" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charlotte Brontë"><a href = vnd.unilang:charlotte.html>Charlotte</a> Brontë</a> |  <a href = vnd.unilang:jill.html>Jill</a> Kriegel, editor, <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jane_Eyre" class="extiw" title="w:Jane Eyre"><a href = vnd.unilang:jane.html>Jane</a> Eyre: With an Introduction and Contemporary Criticism</a></cite> (Ignatius Critical Editions), San Francisco, Calif. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ignatius_Press" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ignatius Press">Ignatius Press</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=x693BwAAQBAJamp;pg=PA569">page 569</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">As a child, <a href = vnd.unilang:jane.html>Jane</a> [Eyre] <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> completely bereft of love, living a loveless existence, which <b>sullies</b> her character. Her emotions are raw and, on the surface, completely out of control.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To become soiled or tarnished.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1730</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Bacon" class="extiw" title="w:Francis Bacon">Francis Bacon</a>,  “The Lord Bacon’s Questions, with <a href = vnd.unilang:dr.html>Dr</a>. Meverel’s Solutions, Concerning the Compounding, Incorporating, or Union of Metals or Minerals; which Subject <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the First Letter of His Lordship’s Alphabet”, in  <cite>The Works of Francis Bacon, <a href = vnd.unilang:baron.html>Baron</a> of Verulam, Viscount St Alban, and Lord High Chancellor of England</cite>, volume III, London |  J. and J. Knapton [<i>et <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>.</i>], <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/926240085">926240085</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=VHNUAAAAYAAJamp;pg=PA215">page 215</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[G]old <a href = vnd.unilang:bears.html>bears</a> the fire, which ſilver doth not: but that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an excellency in nature, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> nothing at all in uſe; for any dignity in uſe I know none, but that ſilvering will <b>ſully</b> and canker more than gilding; <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***suns.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:suns.html>suns</a> (72598)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*šuo</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*šunas</i> (parallel form <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*šuns</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*ś(w)ō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱwṓ</i>, genitive <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱunós</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱunés</i>. An older Latvian form <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">*so</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now found only in one dialect (Nīgrande) as a word to call dogs. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">šuõ</i> (genitive <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">šuñs</i>, dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">šunis</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">sunis</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hundaz</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌷𐌿𐌽𐌳𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hunds</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hundr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">hundur</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">hund</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hunt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hund</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hund</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hound</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Irish language">Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga">cú</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">ci</i>, plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">cŵn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">श्वन्</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">śván</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, genitive <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">शुनस्</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">śunas</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬯𐬞𐬁</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κύων</i> <span href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">cane</i>, <span class="etyl"><a ***supermodel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:supermodel.html>supermodel</a> (20685)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First written example <a href = vnd.unilang:dating.html>dating</a> from 1942 in the English language, in common use since the late 1980s.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Falsely attributed to <a href = vnd.unilang:supermodel.html>supermodel</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Janice_Dickinson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Janice Dickinson">Janice Dickinson</a>, who says she <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Janice_Dickinsonquot;First_supermodelquot;_claim" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Janice Dickinson">coined the term</a> nearly 40 years <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:supermodel.html>supermodel</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">supermodels</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A highly paid, famous fashion model.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">model</span></li></ul>

***supertanker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:supertanker.html>supertanker</a> (99087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">super-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tanker</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:supertanker.html>supertanker</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:supertankers.html>supertankers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An extremely large tanker ship.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to Wikipedia, an oil tanker must have the deadweight of <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> 250,000 tons to qualify as <a href = vnd.unilang:supertanker.html>supertanker</a>. In oil carrying capacity this means about 2 million <a href = vnd.unilang:barrels.html>barrels</a>.
</p>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:suppoost.html>suppoost</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">suppost</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">suppositus</i>.
